<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/bmahee375/djy/blob/master/gb/21/11/1/n13344515.md#1" target="_blank">2人中就有1人曾失眠？两大治疗方法助睡眠</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/bmahee375/djy/blob/master/gb/21/11/1/n13344515.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/11/id13345720-shutterstock_1512086678-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>人为什么会失眠？人体靠着大脑的醒睡系统稳定调控快速动眼期与非快速动眼期，使睡眠有节律，其中环节一旦有些微差错就可能失眠。蓝光、药物、疾病也会造成失眠。治疗失眠分为心理治疗与药物治疗。第一线治疗首推心理治疗，主要以“失眠认知行为治疗”为主，如限眠疗法、放松技巧与睡眠卫生教育。药物治疗则包括各种安眠药及褪黑激素等。......<br><img align="bottom" src="https://www.epochtimes.com/assets/themes/djy/images/time.gif"> 2021年11月03日 2:31 AM			</td></tr>

<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/bmahee375/djy/blob/master/gb/21/11/1/n13344602.md#1" target="_blank">拜登税改提议及应变之道（上）</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/bmahee375/djy/blob/master/gb/21/11/1/n13344602.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/07/id13106401-1-WATaxLawin2021-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>文：林懿?加州会计师
